Automatically classifies tasks into compliance tiers and enforces appropriate verification.\n\n**Key Benefits**:\n- Single command replaces confusion between `sc:task` and `sc:task-mcp`\n- Automatic tier classification with confidence scoring\n- Appropriate verification for each task type\n- Prevents over-engineering for trivial changes\n- Ensures safety for critical changes\n\n## Triggers\n\nUse `/sc:task` when:\n- Task involves code modifications with downstream impacts\n- Complexity score >0.6 with code modifications\n- Multi-file scope (>2 estimated affected files)\n- Security domain paths detected (auth/, security/, crypto/)\n- Refactoring or system-wide changes requested\n\n**Auto-Suggest Keywords**:\n- High confidence: \"implement feature\", \"refactor system\", \"fix security\", \"add authentication\", \"update database schema\"\n- Moderate confidence: \"add new\", \"create component\", \"update service\", \"modify API\"\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\n/sc:task [description]                           # Auto-detect all dimensions\n/sc:task [description] --compliance strict       # Force STRICT tier\n/sc:task [description] --compliance light        # Force LIGHT tier\n/sc:task [description] --skip-compliance         # Bypass compliance (escape hatch)\n/sc:task [description] --verify auto             # Auto-select verification\n```\n\n## Behavioral Flow\n\n### 0. Classification (Already Performed)\n\nClassification was handled by the `/sc:task` command before this skill was invoked. The tier has been determined and the classification header has been emitted. Load context via codebase-retrieval\n2. Search downstream impacts (find_referencing_symbols OR grep)\n3. Make changes\n4. Run affected tests OR document manual verification\n5. Verify basic functionality\n\n**LIGHT Execution**:\n1. Quick scope check (files/lines within bounds)\n2. Make changes\n3. Quick sanity check (syntax valid, no obvious errors)\n4. Proceed with judgment\n\n**EXEMPT Execution**:\n1. Execute immediately\n2. No verification overhead\n\n### 4. Verification Phase\n\nRoute to appropriate verification based on tier and paths:\n\n| Compliance Tier | Verification Method | Token Cost | Timeout |\n|-----------------|---------------------|------------|---------|\n| STRICT | Sub-agent (quality-engineer) | 3-5K | 60s |\n| STANDARD | Direct test execution | 300-500 | 30s |\n| LIGHT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n| EXEMPT | Skip verification | 0 | 0s |\n\n**Critical Path Override**: Paths matching `auth/`, `security/`, `crypto/`, `models/`, `migrations/` always trigger CRITICAL verification regardless of compliance tier.\n\n**Trivial Path Override**: Paths matching `*.md`, `docs/`, `*test*.py` may skip verification.\n\n### 5. Feedback Collection\n\nAfter completion, collect implicit feedback:\n- Track if user overrode tier (implicit classification feedback)\n- Note smooth completion vs errors (quality signal)\n- Store for calibration learning\n\n## MCP Integration\n\n**Required Servers by Tier**:\n- STRICT: Sequential, Serena (fallback not allowed)\n- STANDARD: Sequential, Context7 (fallback allowed)\n- LIGHT: None required (fallback allowed)\n- EXEMPT: None required\n\n**Circuit Breaker Behavior**:\n- If required servers unavailable for STRICT tier, block task execution\n- For other tiers, use fallbacks with noted limitations\n\n## Tool Coordination\n\n**Planning Phase**:\n1. TodoWrite: Create task breakdown\n2. codebase-retrieval: Load context\n3. list_memories / read_memory: Check project state\n\n**Execution Phase**:\n1. Edit/MultiEdit/Write: Make changes\n2. Grep/Glob: Find references\n3. find_referencing_symbols: Trace dependencies\n\n**Verification Phase**:\n1. Task (quality-engineer): Spawn verification agent (STRICT only)\n2. Bash: Run tests directly (STANDARD)\n3. think_about_task_adherence: Reflect on completeness\n\n**Completion Phase**:\n1. write_memory: Save session state\n2. think_about_whether_you_are_done: Final {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_01RtkE4yQVHqaK94LYEbhc9E","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01P6Rg9eXjDQHa1qMPpk2Kqi","name":"mcp__serena__replace_symbol_body","input":{"name_path":"parse_tasklist","relative_path":"src/superclaude/cli/sprint/config.py","body":"def parse_tasklist(content: str, execution_mode: str = \"claude\") -> list[TaskEntry]:\n    \"\"\"Parse phase tasklist markdown into a structured task inventory.\n\n    Extracts task ID, title, dependency annotations, command, and classifier\n    from each ``### T<PP>.<TT> -- Title`` block. Malformed input (missing\n    headings, invalid IDs, empty content) is handled gracefully — invalid\n    blocks are skipped with a logged warning.\n\n    Args:\n        content: Raw markdown text of a phase tasklist file.\n        execution_mode: The phase execution mode (``claude``, ``python``, or\n            ``skip``). When ``python``, every task must have a non-empty\n            ``**Command:**`` field; a :class:`click.ClickException` is raised\n            on the first task found without one.\n\n    Returns:\n        Ordered list of :class:`TaskEntry` instances.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not content or not content.strip():\n        return []\n\n    headings = list(_TASK_HEADING_RE.finditer(content))\n    if not headings:\n        _logger.warning(\"No task headings (### T<PP>.<TT>) found in tasklist content\")\n        return []\n\n    tasks: list[TaskEntry] = []\n    for i, match in enumerate(headings):\n        task_id = match.group(1)\n        title = match.group(2).strip()\n\n        # Extract the block body between this heading and the next (or EOF)\n        block_start = match.end()\n        block_end = headings[i + 1].start() if i + 1 < len(headings) else len(content)\n        block = content[block_start:block_end]\n\n        # Extract dependencies\n        dependencies: list[str] = []\n        dep_match = _DEPENDENCY_RE.search(block)\n        if dep_match:\n            dep_text = dep_match.group(1).strip()\n            if dep_text.lower() not in (\"none\", \"\"):\n                dependencies = _TASK_ID_REF_RE.findall(dep_text)\n\n        # Extract **Command:** field (strip surrounding backticks)\n        command = \"\"\n        cmd_match = _COMMAND_RE.search(block)\n        if cmd_match:\n            command = cmd_match.group(1).strip().strip(\"`\")\n\n        # Extract | Classifier | table row\n        classifier = \"\"\n        cls_match = _CLASSIFIER_RE.search(block)\n        if cls_match:\n            classifier = cls_match.group(1).strip()\n\n        # Build description from the deliverables section if present\n        description = \"\"\n        for line in block.splitlines():\n            stripped = line.strip()\n            if stripped.startswith(\"**Deliverables:**\"):\n                # Grab the next non-empty line(s) after \"Deliverables:\"\n                idx = block.index(stripped) + len(stripped)\n                rest = block[idx:].strip()\n                desc_lines = []\n                for dline in rest.splitlines():\n                    dline = dline.strip()\n                    if not dline or dline.startswith(\"**\"):\n                        break\n                    # Malformed input (missing\n    headings, invalid IDs, empty content) is handled gracefully — invalid\n    blocks are skipped with a logged warning.\n\n    Args:\n        content: Raw markdown text of a phase tasklist file.\n        execution_mode: The phase execution mode (``claude``, ``python``, or\n            ``skip``). {index_path}\")\n\n    phases = discover_phases(index_path)\n    if not phases:\n        raise click.ClickException(\n            \"No phase files discovered. Auto-detect end phase\n    if end_phase == 0:\n        end_phase = max(p.number for p in phases)\n\n    # Validate\n    validation = validate_phases(phases, start_phase, end_phase)\n    errors = validation[\"errors\"]\n    warnings = validation[\"warnings\"]\n    if errors:\n        for e in errors:\n            click.echo(e, err=True)\n        raise click.ClickException(f\"{len(errors)} phase file(s) missing.\")\n\n    for w in warnings:\n        click.echo(w, err=True)\n\n    config = SprintConfig(\n        index_path=index_path,\n        release_dir=index_path.parent,\n        phases=phases,\n        start_phase=start_phase,\n        end_phase=end_phase,\n        max_turns=max_turns,\n        model=model,\n        dry_run=dry_run,\n        permission_flag=permission_flag,\n        debug=debug,\n        stall_timeout=stall_timeout,\n        stall_action=stall_action,\n        shadow_gates=shadow_gates,\n    )\n\n    # Validate that the requested range yields at least one active phase\n    if not config.active_phases:\n        available = [p.number for p in phases]\n        raise click.ClickException(\n            f\"No phases in range [{start_phase}, {end_phase}]. \"\n            f\"Available phase numbers: {available}\"\n        )\n\n    return config\n\n\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n# Tasklist parser — extracts task inventory from phase markdown\n# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n_TASK_HEADING_RE = re.compile(\n    r\"^###\\s+(T\\d{2}\\.\\d{2})\\s*(?:--|-—|—)\\s*(.+)\",\n    re.MULTILINE,\n)\n\n_DEPENDENCY_RE = re.compile(\n    r\"\\*\\*Dependencies:\\*\\*\\s*(.*)\",\n    re.IGNORECASE,\n)\n\n_TASK_ID_REF_RE = re.compile(r\"T\\d{2}\\.\\d{2}\")\n\n# Matches: **Command:** `some command` or **Command:** some command\n_COMMAND_RE = re.compile(\n    r\"\\*\\*Command:\\*\\*\\s*`?([^`\\n]+)`?\",\n    re.IGNORECASE,\n)\n\n# Matches a pipe-table row: | Classifier | value |\n_CLASSIFIER_RE = re.compile(\n    r\"^\\|\\s*Classifier\\s*\\|\\s*([^|]+)\\|\",\n    re.IGNORECASE | re.MULTILINE,\n)\n\n_logger = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.sprint.config\")\n\n\ndef parse_tasklist(content: str, execution_mode: str = \"claude\") -> list[TaskEntry]:\n    \"\"\"Parse phase tasklist markdown into a structured task inventory.\n\n    Extracts task ID, title, dependency annotations, command, and classifier\n    from each ``### T<PP>.<TT> -- Title`` block. Malformed input (missing\n    headings, invalid IDs, empty content) is handled gracefully — invalid\n    blocks are skipped with a logged warning.\n\n    Args:\n        content: Raw markdown text of a phase tasklist file.\n        execution_mode: The phase execution mode (``claude``, ``python``, or\n            ``skip``). When ``python``, every task must have a non-empty\n            ``**Command:**`` field; a :class:`click.ClickException` is raised\n            on the first task found without one.\n\n    Returns:\n        Ordered list of :class:`TaskEntry` instances.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not content or not content.strip():\n        return []\n\n    headings = list(_TASK_HEADING_RE.finditer(content))\n    if not headings:\n        _logger.warning(\"No task headings (### T<PP>.<TT>) found in tasklist content\")\n        return []\n\n    tasks: list[TaskEntry] = []\n    for i, match in enumerate(headings):\n        task_id = match.group(1)\n        title = match.group(2).strip()\n\n        # Extract the block body between this heading and the next (or EOF)\n        block_start = match.end()\n        block_end = headings[i + 1].start() if i + 1 < len(headings) else len(content)\n        block = content[block_start:block_end]\n\n        # Extract dependencies\n        dependencies: list[str] = []\n        dep_match = _DEPENDENCY_RE.search(block)\n        if dep_match:\n            dep_text = dep_match.group(1).strip()\n            if dep_text.lower() not in (\"none\", \"\"):\n                dependencies = _TASK_ID_REF_RE.findall(dep_text)\n\n        # Extract **Command:** field (strip surrounding backticks)\n        command = \"\"\n        cmd_match = _COMMAND_RE.search(block)\n        if cmd_match:\n            command = cmd_match.group(1).strip().strip(\"`\")\n\n        # Extract | Classifier | table row\n        classifier = \"\"\n        cls_match = _CLASSIFIER_RE.search(block)\n        if cls_match:\n            classifier = cls_match.group(1).strip()\n\n        # Build description from the deliverables section if present\n        description = \"\"\n        for line in block.splitlines():\n            stripped = line.strip()\n            if stripped.startswith(\"**Deliverables:**\"):\n                # Grab the next non-empty line(s) after \"Deliverables:\"\n                idx = block.index(stripped) + len(stripped)\n                rest = block[idx:].strip()\n                desc_lines = []\n                for dline in rest.splitlines():\n                    dline = dline.strip()\n                    if not dline or dline.startswith(\"**\"):\n                        break\n                    # Strip leading \"- \" from markdown list items\n                    if dline.startswith(\"- \"):\n                        dline = dline[2:]\n                    desc_lines.append(dline)\n                description = \" \".join(desc_lines)\n                break\n\n        # Validate python-mode tasks have a command (fail fast at parse time)\n        if execution_mode == \"python\" and not command:\n            raise click.ClickException(\n                f\"Task {task_id} in python-mode phase has no command\"\n            )\n\n        tasks.append(\n            TaskEntry(\n                task_id=task_id,\n                title=title,\n                description=description,\n                dependencies=dependencies,\n                command=command,\n                classifier=classifier,\n            )\n        )\n\n    return tasks\n\n\ndef parse_tasklist_file(path: Path) -> list[TaskEntry]:\n    \"\"\"Read a phase tasklist file and parse it into a task inventory.\n\n    Args:\n        path: Path to the phase tasklist markdown file.\n\n    Returns:\n        Ordered list of :class:`TaskEntry` instances.\n\n    Raises:\n        FileNotFoundError: If the path does not exist.\n    \"\"\"\n    content = path.read_text(errors=\"replace\")\n    return parse_tasklist(content)\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":355,"oldLines":11,"newStart":355,"newLines":12,"lines":["     return tasks"," "," ","-def parse_tasklist_file(path: Path) -> list[TaskEntry]:","+def parse_tasklist_file(path: Path, execution_mode: str = \"claude\") -> list[TaskEntry]:","     \"\"\"Read a phase tasklist file and parse it into a task inventory."," ","     Args:","         path: Path to the phase tasklist markdown file.","+        execution_mode: The phase execution mode (passed to :func:`parse_tasklist`)."," ","     Returns:","         Ordered list of :class:`TaskEntry` instances."]},{"oldStart":368,"oldLines":4,"newStart":369,"newLines":4,"lines":["         FileNotFoundError: If the path does not exist.","     \"\"\"","     content = path.read_text(errors=\"replace\")","-    return parse_tasklist(content)","+    return parse_tasklist(content, execution_mode=execution_mode)"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

Malformed input (missing\n    headings, invalid IDs, empty content) is handled gracefully — invalid\n    blocks are skipped with a logged warning.\n\n    Args:\n        content: Raw markdown text of a phase tasklist file.\n        execution_mode: The phase execution mode (``claude``, ``python``, or\n            ``skip``). When ``python``, every task must have a non-empty\n            ``**Command:**`` field; a :class:`click.ClickException` is raised\n            on the first task found without one.\n\n    Returns:\n        Ordered list of :class:`TaskEntry` instances.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not content or not content.strip():\n        return []\n\n    headings = list(_TASK_HEADING_RE.finditer(content))\n    if not headings:\n        _logger.warning(\"No task headings (### T<PP>.<TT>) found in tasklist content\")\n        return []\n\n    tasks: list[TaskEntry] = []\n    for i, match in enumerate(headings):\n        task_id = match.group(1)\n        title = match.group(2).strip()\n\n        # Extract **Command:** field (strip surrounding backticks)\n        command = \"\"\n        cmd_match = _COMMAND_RE.search(block)\n        if cmd_match:\n            command = cmd_match.group(1).strip().strip(\"`\")\n\n        # Extract | Classifier | table row\n        classifier = \"\"\n        cls_match = _CLASSIFIER_RE.search(block)\n        if cls_match:\n            classifier = cls_match.group(1).strip()\n\n        # Build description from the deliverables section if present\n        description = \"\"\n        for line in block.splitlines():\n            stripped = line.strip()\n            if stripped.startswith(\"**Deliverables:**\"):\n                # Grab the next non-empty line(s) after \"Deliverables:\"\n                idx = block.index(stripped) + len(stripped)\n                rest = block[idx:].strip()\n                desc_lines = []\n                for dline in rest.splitlines():\n                    dline = dline.strip()\n                    if not dline or dline.startswith(\"**\"):\n                        break\n                    # Strip leading \"- \" from markdown list items\n                    if dline.startswith(\"- \"):\n                        dline = dline[2:]\n                    desc_lines.append(dline)\n                description = \" \".join(desc_lines)\n                break\n\n        #
